**GT:** `11.119*epsilon^2 + 11.119*epsilon*(-0.0920*(T - 352.008) + 1) + 4.370*(T - 352.008)*log(epsilon + 1)`

Let me first expand the GT:
- `11.119*epsilon^2 + 11.119*epsilon - 11.119*0.0920*epsilon*(T - 352.008) + 4.370*(T - 352.008)*log(epsilon + 1)`
- `= 11.119*epsilon^2 + 11.119*epsilon - 1.0226*epsilon*T + 1.0226*352.008*epsilon + 4.370*T*log(epsilon+1) - 4.370*352.008*log(epsilon+1)`

Simplifying:
- `= 11.119*epsilon^2 - 1.0226*epsilon*T + (11.119 + 359.96)*epsilon + 4.370*T*log(epsilon+1) - 1538.3*log(epsilon+1)`
- `= 11.119*epsilon^2 - 1.0226*T*epsilon + 371.08*epsilon + 4.370*T*log(epsilon+1) - 1538.3*log(epsilon+1)`

So GT has the structure: **a*epsilon^2 + b*T*epsilon + c*epsilon + d*T*log(epsilon+1) + e*log(epsilon+1)**

Now let me check candidates for this structure:

**Candidate 68:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon + c2*log(c3*epsilon + 1) + c4*log(c5*epsilon + 1)`
This gives T*epsilon, epsilon, and two log terms but no epsilon^2. **No match.**

**Candidate 69:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon + c2*log(c3*epsilon + 1) + c4*epsilon/(c5*epsilon + c6) + c7/(c5*epsilon + c6)`
Has T*epsilon, epsilon, log terms, and rational terms but no epsilon^2. **No match.**

**Candidate 85:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon + c2*log(c3*epsilon + 1) + c4*epsilon*exp(c5/T)`
This has T-dependent exponential, not matching. **No match.**

**Candidate 63:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon + c2*log(c3*epsilon + 1) + c4*epsilon*log(T*c5 + 1)`
Structure: T*epsilon, epsilon, log(epsilon+1), epsilon*log(T*c5+1). The GT needs T*log(epsilon+1), not epsilon*log(T). **No match.**

**Candidate 1:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon + c2*log(c3*epsilon + 1) + c4*epsilon^c5*log(c6*epsilon + 1)`
Setting c5=0: c4*log(c6*epsilon+1), giving two log terms plus T*epsilon + epsilon. No epsilon^2 and no T*log term. But if c5=1: c4*epsilon*log(c6*epsilon+1). Still no T*log. **No match.**

**Candidate 19:** `T*c0*epsilon + T^c1*c2*epsilon^c3 + c4*epsilon + c5*log(c6*epsilon + 1)`
Setting c1=1, c3=0: T*c0*epsilon + T*c2 + c4*epsilon + c5*log(...). No, need T*log(epsilon+1). Setting c1=1, c3=0 gives constant*T, not T*log. **No match.**

**Candidate 27:** `T^c0*c1*epsilon^c2 + c3*epsilon^c4 + c5*epsilon + c6*log(c7*epsilon+1)`
Setting c0=1,c2=1: T*c1*epsilon. But need T*log(epsilon+1) too. **No match.**

**Candidate 38:** `c0*epsilon^c1 + c2*epsilon^c3*exp(T*c4) + c5*epsilon^c6*log(c7*epsilon+1)`
This has exp(T*c4) which is exponential in T, not linear. **No match** (unless c4=0, but then no T dependence at all).
